0 CHANGES~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
   {R}                      New and Old Changes to MPV2/VoR
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{G}Last updated 04/20/06
{N}
- New guilds {R}(Kilith){N}
  - {B}Marauder {N}a multi warrior/thief guild - {B}Elementals {N}a multi healer/wizard guild
  - {B}Paladin {N}a multi warrior/healer guild - {B}Battlemage {N}a multi warrior/wizard guild
  - {B}Necromancer {N}this is a raise undead guild. {C}All guilds in game{N}
{N}
- Tracks will no longer log! They will fade as time goes by. {R}(Eraser){N}
- A reroller has been added to character creation {R}(Eraser){N}
- A NEW remort system is now implemented. {R}(Kenor){B} see help remort!{N}
- New skills have been added: Dual Backstab and Second Kick {R}(Kenor){N}
- Racial stat limits now 35! {R}(Eraser) {B}see help races! {N}
- Bags hit by acid will not disolve eq inside. It will be returned to your inventory! {R}(Eraser){N}
- config eqlist --> Will sort your eqlist with only eq worn, eq worn (head to toe)
                    eq with empty slots show, and eq with empty slots shown (head to toe) {R}(Eraser){N}
- Added: Kneepads, Elbowpads, Eyepatch, and Back eq slots & addaffect mana {R}(Kilith){N}

As of Febuary 2006

- Added in new skills of:
- Charge - Paladin skill {R}See help charge{N}
- Shield Rush - Paladin skill {R}See help shield rush{N}
- Calm - Paladin skill {R}See help Calm{N}
- Vampiric Bite - Necromancer skill {R}See help Vampiric Bite{N}
- Stab - Thief and Marauder skill {R}See Help Stab{N}
- Second Kick - Warrior Skill {R}See Help Second Kick{N}
- Dual Backstab - Thief/Assassin Skill {R}See help Dual Backstab
- Warcry - Warrior Skill - {R}See help Warcry{N}

New eq type:

- Lance - This was made for Paladin eq. It is needed to use charge.
- Plus Backstab eq - This is used to a thief style type eq to raise backstab and stab
                     damage. It does not affect circle damage.
- Plus mana eq - This will add mana to your character ontop of mana added by gems.
- Death Mana - This a new type of mana introduced to the game. This will be used for
               Necromancer spells. Gem will be made for this mana type.

As of April 2006
- New Guilds {R}(Kilith){N}
  - {B}Tatics {N}This is a new guild that adds to Warrior type guilds.{N}
  - {B}Shaman {N}This is a new guild that adds to Healer type guilds.{N}
  - {B}Mystics {N}This is a new guild that adds to Wizard type guilds.{N}

{R}                           New Player Help File
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

{N}Welcome to {B}Midpoint Void 2{N}/{R}Void of Reality The New Beginning.{N}

In this help file we will explain some of the basic commands to help you get
started on the mud. This mud might be very different from other muds you have 
played. Why you may as. What are the differences?

We have 2 different alignments Good (whities) and Evil (darkies).
Each alignment has its own chats. Chat, raid, and  act <auction>.
You may need to be of certin level to use some of these channels. 
Chat everyone has. Once you have gained enough levels there is also
an X-Chat which is an across alignment chat.

Q. Can you have Multiple characters?
A. No! If you are caught with two players one will be deleted. I check logs daily
       And if I see that a player has a lot of new warpoints I will look for any
       signs of cheating. We have an on mud logsearch. We will find out.

To help you out with what differs mobs and players and objects in rooms. 
I will put them below as if you were looking in a room.

Example of a mob:
{C}A high elf stand here to protect the newbie area. {G}(Sanctuary){N}

Example of a same alignment player:
{P}Kilith is standing here.{N}
{P}Sabelis is flying. {G}(Sanctuary){N}

Example of an Opposite alignment player:
{P}+* A High-elf *+ is flying.{N}
{P}+* A Wild-Elf *+ is here.{N}

Object on the ground:
{c}a old rusty sword lies on the ground.{N}

{B}Basic Commands{N}:
{G}CONSIDER{N}               - Use consider when you are thinking about killing a mob.
                         This will help you see if the mob will kill you or not.
{G}KILL <MOB/PLAYER>{N}      - This will make you attack a mob or player.
{G}LOOK{N}                   - This command just makes you see what is in a room.
{G}WHO{N}                    - This will show you who is on the mud. - Level 15
                         Why is it level 15? So that no one can roll and cheat and
                         see who is on the other side.
{G}LEARN{N}                  - When you are at a teacher type learn to see what they teach
{G}LEARN <SKILL/SPELL>{N}    - This will make you learn the skill or spell
{G}PRACTICE     {N}          - This works with learn. This will help you become more
                         proficient in your spell or skill.
{G}PRACTICE <SKILL/SPELL>{N} - This will raise your skill level on skills
                         and on spells.
{G}CHAT  {N}                 - Lets you talk to players on your alignment side.
{G}PRAY   {N}                - It is a way for you to talk with immortals without everyone
                         on your side hearing you talk to us.
{G}FOLLOW <players name>{N}  - This command is how you follow another player of your alignment.
{G}SPAM     {N}              - What this command does is change how things in rooms look.
type spam to toggle through    Like players with affects. 
                               SPAM
                               A high elf stand here to protect the newbie area.
                               ...skin hard as stone.
                               ...a high elf is protected by a bright aura!
                               NO SPAM
                    A high elf stand here to protect the newbie area. (Stoneskin) (Sanctuary)

There are a few of the commands to help you get started on this mud.

{R}Also see help files:

{B}HELP PK
HELP MUDMAP
HELP DARKIE
HELP WHITIE
HELP XYLAR
HELP MASQE

{N}I also added the max for each type of armor I want to try for each
metal. Also the color of each metal will match the colors they are here.

{Y}REMEMBER WHEN DOING WHITE IN YOUR WEAPON OR ARMOR COLORS USE $N$7 IF YOU
DO NOT USE $N$7 FOR SOME PLAYERS THE WHITE YOU MIGHT SEE WILL BE GREEN TO
OTHERS. THE PRIMARY COLOR FOR TEXT ON ZMUD IS GREEN. THE PRIMARY COLOR FOR
TELNET, WINTIN, AND SOME OF THE OTHER PROGRAMS ARE ANSI SO TEXT IS WHITE.
SO TO MAKE THIS:{N}(I SHOULD ADD FOR BRIGHT WHITE.... HEH NOT MUCH
DIFFERENCE.... USE $B$7.)
{R}Please also remember that at the end of each item put a $N. If you do not add this
all of us admins will be fixing all your bleeding ansi and that is not fun to do
if you have alot of color in your item.

{W}THIS IS $B$7 {C}LIKE I SAID VERY SMALL COLOR DIFFERENCE.
{w}THIS IS $N$7

{R}Weight for certin metal and other meterial types for armor      

{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{N}   {R}body armor        Armor Ratings by locations
{R}       weight: body: head: Arms: Hands: Legs: Feet: Shoulder: Shield:
{Y}Gold{N}     8       8     6     6     7      5     5      7      H-2 B-5 A-5 L-2
{d}Iron{N}    10       6     5     5     6      4     4      6      H-2 B-4 A-4 L-2
{c}Steel{N}    5       5     4     4     5      3     3      5      H-1 B-3 A-3 L-1
{d}Silver{N}   4       4     3     3     4      2     2      4      H-1 B-2 A-2 L-1
{y}Copper{N}   3       3     2     2     3      1     1      3      H-1 B-1 A-1 L-1
{y}Leather{N}  2       2     1     1     2      1     1      2      H-0 B-1 A-1 L-0
{y}Cloth{N}    1       1     1     1     1      1     1      1      ***************
{y}Wood{N}     1       *     *     1     1      *     1      1      H-0 B-1 A-1 L-0




   {B}METAL:          DURIBILITY  COSTS: in copper    
   {Y}GOLD{N} NONMAGICAL:   20-24    {c}2500+          {Y}GOLD {B}MAGICAL:  21-25 {c}3000+
   {d}IRON{N} NONMAGICAL:   16-20    {c}2000-2500      {d}IRON {B}MAGICAL:  17-21 {c}2500-3000
  {c}STEEL{N} NONMAGICAL:   12-16    {c}1500-2000     {c}STEEL {B}MAGICAL:  13-17 {c}2000-2500
 {d}SILVER{N} NONMAGICAL:   10-12    {c}1000-1500    {d}SILVER {B}MAGICAL:  11-13 {c}1500-2000
 {y}COPPER{N} NONMAGICAL:   8-10     {c}500-1000     {y}COPPER {B}MAGICAL:  9-11  {c}1000-1500
{y}LEATHER{N} NONMAGICAL:   6-8      {c}100-500     {y}LEATHER {B}MAGICAL:  7-9   {c}500-1000
  {y}CLOTH{N} NONMAGICAL:   4-6      {c}1-100         {y}CLOTH {B}MAGICAL:  5-7   {c}100-500
   {y}WOOD{N} NONMAGICAL:   3-4      {c}1-100          {y}WOOD {B}MAGICAL:  4-5   {c}100-500{N}

Duribility is your v6 and v7 Make sure v6 is one of these numbers compared to what
type of Metal you have used. v7 should at least be a 1, if it is a 0 the item will be
broken and can not be fixed. v7 should usally be the same as v6 but does not have to be
as long as v7 is > 0. Also put the type of metal you picked out to you
in the name part of your item. AKA you have a Breastplate of Anger. You made 
the breastplate out of silver on this table. Make sure you put NAME SILVER BREASTPLATE
OF ANGER in your name field.
If the armor is none magical then use these values. If the armor is
magical as in glow or hum... Then you can suptract 2 from weight and
can add 1 to armor rating. So like for body armor that is Iron and magical
weight would be 8 and armor rating would go from 6 to 7. 

Also see: OEDIT, WEAPONS,

{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{N}syntax: delete character forever

{R}NUMBER ONE RULE IF IS YOU DELETE YOU DO NOT GET A REIMBURSEMENT!
{N}If you get killed and delete out of anger that is your choice. The best
thing to do when you get angry is to log off take some time. Then from
there log back on after cooling off. Log on after cooling off and rebuild
your kit from friends and popping eq. EQ is easy to get the levels and
remorts are not.

{R}NUMBER TWO RULE:
{N}You can not delete if you have gained one remort. You must ask an admin
to lower your remorts to zero to delete. This is to prevent pk death deletions.

{G}On homeland mobs (level 1-65):{N}
No weapon will go over the max of 10 damage. 1d10 2d5 5d2 10d2

{R}On mobs from level 66-101{N}
Weapon damage range from 11-18. 2d8 8d2 2d9 9d2 18d1 1d18 3d5 5d3 ect...

{C}On ELITE MOBS!!! level 102-200:{N}
Weapon damage can range from 19-25 

{R}Warning not many of these weapons will be in the mud!! To make a weapon
of this damage you must ask Kilith for permission!!!{N}

{B}GEMS!!!{N}

{R}No GEMS{N} are to be created unless you have asked for permission from
Kilith. Any {R}GEMS{N} found will be deleted if made with out my OK. 
If you want a gem made. Make the gem, tell me the vnum, type of mana and I will make it.

{R}NO CHEATER EQ WHAT SO EVER!!! If you make it you will be punished.{N}
1st offence builder forzen one day!
2nd offence builder loss of levels (if you are 103 baned from mud one day)
{N}3rd offence builder deleted and area removed from the mud.

{B}Armor APB max will be +1 on all eq wear locations.{N} We have 25 wear
locations, so that will be a max of 25 APB on all your EQ! IF YOU MAKE APB
EQ YOU MUST PUT IN THE NAME OF THE ITEM APB so we can search for APB items
with OFIND APB.{N}

{B}PLUS STAT ITEMS: 
{R}There is to be NO PLUS STAT ITEMS IN THE GAME WHAT SO EVER!{N}

{B}Alignments on mobs:{N}
With the playing of alignments on mobs I have noticed:
from {R}-120 to -130{N} would raise someone of {B}good alignment {R}1{N} point.
from {R}-140 to -200{N} would raise someone of {B}good alignment {R}2{N} points.
from {R}-210 to -999{N} would raise someone of {B}good alignment {R}3{N} points.

The way this works is a good aligned mob will lower the alignment of a
good aligned player. So if the mob has 500 alignment that player will go
from 1000 alignment to 997 alignment. If they kill a mob with the
alignment of -500 they would then raise 3 points from 997 to 1000 once
again. If you have any questions on what the alignments should be on your
mobs ask an admin.
 

We are going to be talking about eq max, weapon max, mob max all week. so
watch for the max on this stuff in the next few days.

{G}lvl 90  {R}215816 {N}experience
{G}lvl 95  {R}319428 {N}experience
{G}lvl 100 {R}321100 {N}experience
{G}lvl 101 {R}441390 {N}experience
{g}
Level 101 Will be the top xp mob level no other XP mob will be over 101.
Exceptions for this level restriction are:
Mobs that load Powerful eq or weapons.
I will check the mobs that will load eq and depending on the eq will
I except if the mob is to buff/ just right/ or to weak.

Your xp mobs are to your decision...
{R}*by no means are any 86+ mobs in home lands* homeland xp will not
be easy no more then a max of around 10 to 20 85 level mobs in home lands.*{g}

{R}*DO NOT ADJUST EXP ON MOBS BY NO MEANS!!!*{g}
if I catch anyone making the xp of a mob higher I will be upset.
you {G}CAN{g} adjust {G}HP{g} to make it higher but not lower!
to adjust hp type hp <numb> ok hp 10 is normal hp. hp 15 is 1.5 times normal hp
it can go upto a max of 30... {R}please don't use 30 will take people forever to
kill the mob.{g}

{G}*Alignment*{g} Please set the alignment on mobs... if the mob is of {B}good alignment
set alignment to 300 to 700{g}
if the mob is {R}evil set it from -300 to -700{g}

{G}*Cash*{g} please don't give out more then 2 gold on a mob or: syntax: money 200
if the mob is in home lands.... You should almost go by the mobs level
if the mob is level 20 then money 20
this is only homeland policy!!! if the mob is in an xp area in the world you can
go by 10* the mobs level do if the mob is level 400 then money 4000 which is
40 gold. but please don't make many 40 gold mobs...

110 'BATTLEGROUND SETUP'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                          How to setup a Battle Ground
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
To setup a bg is very easy.

See if the who list looks some whateven... if not put a crappy item for prize

All you do is type:

setlevel <level range of 1-90> <prize vnum> <prize vnum>

So

setlevel 1 90 37 37

levels are lvl 1 - 90 and prize is object 37 or a loaf of bread

0 PREREQ PREREQUISITE PREREQUISITES~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                            PREREQUISITE
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

A prerequisite is a skill that you must be proficient in before the
desired skill can be obtained.  Use the prereq <spell/skillname> to see
what prerequisites are required to learn that spell/skill.  You must have
moderate to good proficiency in a prerequisite (50% success level).

{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 BATTLE BATTLEGROUND~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                             BATTLEGROUND
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
The battleground is a 20 square area where you can fight against anyone
in the area with no equipment or experience loss.  Often, a prize will be
awarded to the player left standing when everyone else has died.  Type
battleground to sign up for the battleground once a god announces that it
will begin shortly.

If you win a BG you might gain either 1 or 2 prizes and you will 
gain 5 warpoints.

See also: Help Arena
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 RATING RATINGS~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                             RATING
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

Ratings are based on tons of things:  from the average damage you do to
your stats, to how many times you have died, to if you are on the topten, to
how many and what skills and spells you know.. the algo follows:

rating = ((100-armor_class)/3) + Total_of_all_stats +
         (average_weapon_dam * 5) + (max_hps / 40) +
         (30 points if on topten) + (max_mana / 5) + (level * 1.5) +
         (parry_percent / 18) + (dodge_percent / 18) + (hitroll / 4) +
         (damage_bonus) - (total_deaths / 2)

I'm NOT going to change it, this is for your information only. :)
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 ARENA~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                                   ARENA
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
The arena is a place where any two players can duke it out without worrying
about exp loss or equipment loss from death.  When one player wins, both
players will be transported back to where they were, with their full amount
of hit points.  You may bet on the fights before they begin by typing
bet # <amount> (see help bet for more info or type bet alone for more
options).  Winnings are proportionate to how much you bet... if you bet
1 coin, and the odds are 2 to 1, you will only win 2 coins back.  If you
bid 5000, you will get a bigger chunk of the pool or every bidders' money,
but it may not be a big increase if you did not bid much.  No money is
created; the total money is simply split between the winners depending
on how much they bet.

To configure challenges on/off or arena spam on/middle/off, use config
Arena and config Challenge.  Type Config alone to see how.

See Also: HELP CHALLENGE, HELP BET, HELP ACCEPT, HELP DECLINE.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 ACCEPT~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Once you have been challenged to an arena battle, if you are at full
hitpoints you can accept the challenge.  Accept alone will show who you
will be fighting against, and Accept YES will actually go ahead and
get the fight and betting system set up.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 DECLINE~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Use decline YES to decline an arena challenge from a player.  You can
also configure challenges off by using CONFIG.  Type config alone for
additional info on how to configure arena options.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 BET~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
To bet on the winner of an arena battle, type BET # <amount> where amount
is the number of COPPER coins and # is the person you are betting on
(when the fighters are set, it will say fighter #1 <name> and fighter #2
<name>)  # can only be 1 or 2.  If you lose the bet, you will not get any
money back, and it will notify you that your fighter has lost.  If you
win, the total pool of money of the winners and losers will be divided by
the winners.  If you are a fighter, you MUST bet on yourself if you want
to get some money.. and no, you can't bet on the other guy :P
Note: All money comes out/goes into your bank account.

Type CONFIG to view options you can turn on/off.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 REMORT REMORTING TRANSFORM~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                  {R}REMORTING 
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{N}At certain levels of experience you have a choice: you can continue onward
towards higher levels or you may choose to {W}REMORT{N}.
When your character remorts you gain certain bonuses and penalties:
   
{R}1.{N}  5 extra "points" which can be distributed to stats of choice,
    although none may exceed your races natural stat limits.
{R}2.{N}  Besides the 5 extra stat points you can also choose to up your mana, hp,
    moves, practices, or apb.
{R}3.{N}  You start again at level 1, but with greatly increased hit points, and
    all of your equipment.
{R}4.{N}  You gain 1 maximum skill, and 2 maximum spells.
{R}5.{N}  The second time you remort, you will also never need to eat food, and
    the third time will make you never need to drink.

Be warned, the high levels required to remort are not easily obtained, and
neither in the case of the 2nd, 3rd, 4th, 5th and 6th remorts are the war 
points. When you remort your character is sent back to level 1 and even with
the bonuses you gain it will take quite a while to get back up to high level
again.

The maximum number of remorts on this mud is 7.

Syntax: 
Transform {W}<{B}stat{W}> <{B}stat{W}> <{B}stat{W}> <{B}stat{W}> <{B}stat> {W}<{B}dam{W}/{B}hp{W}/{B}prac{W}/{B}mana{W}/{B}move{W}>{N}
          {B}You can also use {W}<{B}none{W}> {B}as a choice insted of a stat. 
          This is to help if you might go over race limits when remorting.{N}  

Example: Transform str str str con con dam

This will add 3 strength and 2 constitution +2 apb to your character.

{B}dam{N}  =  2 extra attack power bonus
{B}prac{N} = 40 extra practices to start with
{B}hp{N}   = 30 extra hitpoints to start with
{B}move{N} = 25 extra movement points to start with
{B}mana{N} = 15 extra natural mana

{R}SEE HELP REMORT COST {N}for cost on remorting.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 WARPOINTS WAR POINTS 'WAR POINTS' WARPOINT~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
These points are a good indicated of how successful you have been
in the war between good and evil.  Player kills of opposite alignment
add a certain amount of warpoints, depending on their level.  If
you are one of the top ten killers in the lands, then your name will
go on the topten list (view topten list by typing topten).  As a top
killer, you do not recieve anything special per se, except perhaps
the respect and fear of other players.  The difference between
killpoints and warpoints is that warpoints represent player kills,
while killpoints include difficult mob kills.
{R}See: Help Remort and help Remort Cost
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 STORY STORYLINE~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                  {R}Story
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
PAST:
	In the days before history itself, back in the days of the 
ancients, thegreat men of magic ruled the world.  One power hungry 
mage by the nameof Bythus soon declared himself leader by banishing 
seven good ancients intothe netherworld, with one incredible spell.  
As Bythus' power grew, he beganu sing slaves to build a great city.  
Bythar was founded as the first city as a tribute to the great tyrant 
Bythus.  Soon after, the remaining good mages began to fear Bythus 
and did all they could to banish him, but to no avail.  The leader 
of this movement, Kryalis, was turned into a ghost and is rumored 
to still haunt the ancient areas of Bythar that exist today.  Bythus 
created orcs and dark elves as his minions with the help of the dark 
lord, Krag, in order to destroy the opposing ancients. However, in a 
final attempt to stop the imposing doom upon the world, the ancients 
joined together to reign destruction upon the city of Bythar. By an 
incredible fluke of nature, Bythus happened to be sleeping in his
private home in Bythar at the time, and was crushed under the slave-girl
he was sleeping with at the time (and about 10 tons of stone, too).

	Soon after, the remaining ancients built the great city of Xylar 
upon the ancient ruins where Bythar had been.  Before its completion, the 
massive hordes of orcs and magic-throwing dark elves, led by Krag himself, 
charged into the city, slaughtering all in their path.  Krag personally 
snapped the neck of every ancient that stood to defend the city, and in 
no time the city was again in ruins.  Krag became sick of the pleasant flowers
and grasses that seemed to grow wild around the ruins of Xylar, and began
to fear whatever or whoever controlled nature itself, and left back to the 
caves of Masqe with his great horde. 

 However, on his way back, a woman dressed in pure white robes walked slowly 
towards him, staring at him with an intense gaze.  Krag struck the woman down 
with his great staff, but not one second after he had smashed her to the ground, 
his staff turned into a massive serpent and swallowed Krag whole.  With the great 
magic of the world apparently dead, all that was left of magic in the world were 
the few disciples of the ancients and a few stray dark elves.  Legends say that 
the only true powerful magic resides in a strange dimension mortals call Midpoint Void.  
Since the great disappearance of magic, no one has reached the power or understanding 
that the ancient beings of old had wielded, and the land continues to be ruled
by the sword until the one true prophet comes from the midpoint void, and restores 
the ancients' name and magic.

        The world was at peace for 200 years without the gift of magic to corrupt 
the souls of the mortal realm, the world lived by the sword. Until one day, when 
the city of Xylar began to grow dimmer, and the aura that once surrounded the 
city began to fade away. The rumors of a great force beneath the streets of Xylar 
once again became the talk of the world. Then one day, a dark mist fell upon
the city of Xylar totally hiding it from view. The towers of Xylar that use to 
be visible from anywhere in the world were now gone without a trace.
       
	 Rumors that Bythus was awake filled the mortal world with fear. So 
once again the descendants of the seven ancients gathered together to bind 
Bythus beneath the city. However, the use of magic had long been forgotten 
and Bythus simply killed each ancient one by one. Destroying cities, and 
rearranging the world into his New Kingdom. Asmovia, from the city of Marabella 
was the last descendant of the ancients and thus Bythus wanted her dead.  
Bythus summoned her to his castle in Xylar and released all of his hatred upon her.  
In the last moments of her life, she called upon all of forces of nature and
life to summon all the magical powers surrounding New Xylar and bound it to one room... 
The Void of Reality. Throughout the world everyone could hear her death cry as the 
mist slowly lifted and the sun slowly set... Magic was again released into the world. 
The beliefs of legends were brought back through ancestral storytelling and books that 
were passed on. The gods once again came back into belief as this old civilization 
grew once again. The land was devastated, but the towns were built in the areas less
radiated and kings and barrens rule this now destroyed land. The Once great 
Midpoint Void lives to be found again by the mortals, and the mortals still await the 
day they can defeat Bythus and avenge the 7 ancients who delivered them from their 
suffering.

	Not more then a 300 years later, Bythus released himself from the 
Void of Reality. Xylar was in total shock to find out that Bythus once again 
wandered the world. Not more then a few days after the news of the escape of Bythus, 
Xylar was once again surrounded in a dark mist. This time the world knew of magic
and knew how to use this power. Many wizards grouped up to cast a spell to once and 
for all destroy Bythus. After the spell was cast the world seem to change. The spell 
that the wizards cast to destroy Bythus did just that, but it also destroyed the 
known world. Most of Xylar lay in ruins most under a great ocean. Masque and the 
mountain it was built into was almost totally destroyed and now lays in ruins. The 
ghosts of the population of masque have been heard to still inhabit it. The world 
has now begun to rebuild itself. The struggle of good verses evil continues till 
this day with the use of power and magic. Evil will not rest until the death of 
Bythus has been avenged. So this beings us to the Void of Reality the New Beginning!

they were when you last killed him/her and how many times you have killed
the player.  Playerkills in the same alignment will not show up on this
list, nor will mobs.  If all the slots are filled, the lowest level
character will be checked, and if the current kill is of higher level,
the lowest character on the chart will be overwritten.

102 weaponvalues weaponsvalues weapval weaponvalue~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
   {R}                        Weapon Values
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{N}These are the v0-v9 that you see on weapons.

{R}v1 {N}0 = unbreakable, or <damage> (for instance v1 10 means if the 
      weapon does >10 damage it has a chance to dent).            

{R}v3: Weapon attack appearance type:
{R}1{N} = slice
{R}2{N} = stab
{R}3{N} = slash
{R}4{N} = whip
{R}5{N} = claw
{R}7{N} = pound
{R}8{N} = crush
{R}9{N} = gore
{R}11{N} = pierce ** Must be set for weapons that will backstab.

{R}v7{N} . Number of dice rolls.
{R}v8{N} . Number of sides on the dice.
{N}
Eg: v7 2 v8 5 would be 2d5 or 2 rolls of a 5 sided
die. This means the weapon can do 2-10 dam.

0 ALIGNMENT ALIGN~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
On Midpoint Void, good and evil are at war.  Most evil creatures have
been banished from the earth, however there are still some who follow the
ways of evil.  If you are good and you encounter an evil player, you will
not see thier name.  You will simply see +* An Evil xxxx *+ (xxxx being
the race name).  It goes exactly the same for an evil person looking at a
good person.  Guards in good cities kill evil, and guards in evil cities
kill good.  It is an all-out war... Invasions by large groups are
possible.  You are not allowed to group with players of opposite
alignment.  Due to difficulty reasons, neutral players are treated like
they are "good" until they become totally evil.  Player killing between
good and evil results in HUGE amount of experience (depending on the
player level).  Good and evil players do not share the same channels of
communication, but good and evil players both hear YELLS (while in same
zone).  If you become evil while you are in a good town, you either have
to 1. run past the guards or 2. get good again.  If you become evil/good
you will start in the corresponding starting rooms for good/evil.  (IE,
an evil dwarf will go to the evil caves when he dies).  Orcs and
Darkelves can never become good.  That's all for now :P
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 OFFENSE 'OFFENSIVE BONUS' OFFENSIVE~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
-Offensive Bonus-

This bonus is an indicator of how accurately you hit opponents.  It is
based on you dexterity, your level, and your skill with the weapon you are
currently using.  The higher the number the better.

SEE ALSO: ATTACK POWER BONUS, EVASION BONUS
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

0 'ATTACK POWER BONUS' 'ATTACK BONUS' ATTACK~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
-Attack Power Bonus-
-APB-

This bonus is an indicator of the extra damage you do when you hit an
opponent.  It is based on your strength and occassionally on some of the
equipment you are wearing.  Magical weapons also may raise this bonus.
Just because you have an attack power bonus of 8 does not mean you do
8 extra damage per hit; it is an indicator only.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 EVASION 'EVASION BONUS'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
-Evasion Bonus-

This bonus is an indicator of how well you are able to avoid attacks.
Dexterity, Level, Parry-skill, Dodge-skill, and ShieldBlock-skill all
affect this number.  The higher the better (the less you get hit).
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

0 FIGHT OPTIONS 'FIGHT OPTIONS'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: Fight or Fight <togglename>

Typing the word fight by itself will show you a list of your behaviors
in combat and groundfighting.  Typing fight followed by an option will
toggle option on/off.  For instance "fight elbow" would toggle whether or
not I use elbows in groundfighting.  Here is a brief description of some
of the normal fight toggles:

POWER:       If on, your attacks will do slightly more damage.  If off, you
             will be able to attack at a slightly increased speed.
AGGRESSIVE:  If on, your attacks will be more forceful and hit more often.
             If off, you will ocassionally dodge a blow that you might not
             have if aggresive had been on.
GROUND:      If on, you won't try to resist a fight that may end up on the
             ground.  If off, you will do everything in your power to make
             sure the fight doesn't go to the ground.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 REPAIR~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: Repair <item/all>
        Repair <item/all> yes

Certain people in the world, often weaponsmiths or armorers, can
repair damaged weapons and/or armor.  Repair <item> will give you an
estimate of how much the item will cost to repair.  Some magical or
powerful items cannot be repaired at all, and some items may cost more
than others to repair.  If you wish the repairs to be done, type Repair
<item> yes, and the repairer will go ahead and fix up your item.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

0 FLURRY~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: Flurry

Flurry is not a skill that is taught. It is a skill everyone knows how
to do by picking up a stick and waving it around in the air. Flurry is 
a combat skill that allows you to flail about madly in a wild flurry.  
Because of the extreme energies required to go berserk like this, you 
will end up losing many stamina points.  So...  if you are planning to 
run after the battle, this is not a good option.  Anyone can flurry with 
or without a weapon.

0 'KICK'~
{W}Kick
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{N}Level : {W}12
{N}Preqs : {p}None
{N}Guilds: {C}None
{N}Syntax: Kick <victim> or in combat, just Kick



This skill allows you to kick an opponent, inflicting extra damage during
combat.  After you have kicked, you usually are a little off-balance and
it takes 1-3 rounds to recover well enough to cast, flee or perform
another kick.  The power of your kick depends on your level; at low
levels kick is next to useless, at high levels it can be invaluable.

It is impossible to kick ghosts or flying opponents for obvious reasons.

Taught at: {B}Good{N} - Chuck
           {R}Evil{N} - Fiko

0 BASH~
{W}Bash
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{N}Level : {W}9
{N}Preqs : {p}None
{N}Guilds: {C}None
{N}

Syntax: bash <victim> or in combat, just bash

This skill allows you to attempt to push an opponent backwards forcefully
and rapidly, causing them to fall to the ground.  If successful, the
victim will not be able to attack for 2-4 rounds (only defend).

NOTE: Also, it is obviously futile to bash a dragon or a ghost.

Success of bashing is based on how well you have practiced bash, your
strength, and the victim's dexterity and dodge ability.
NOTE: With this skill it is possible that you fall on top of your victim,
in which case you will begin to groundfight, so IF YOU WANT TO AVOID
GROUNDFIGHTING AT ALL COSTS, DON'T BASH!!!!

SEE ALSO: GROUNDFIGHTING

Taught at: {B}Good{N} - Mayor of Xylar - Xylar
           {R}Evil{N} - Sloth - Masqe
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 TACKLE~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
This is am automatic skill, soon to become a real skill.

This command will allow you to run at an opponent, trying to tackle
him/her/it and take them to the ground.  If successful, you will go into
groundfighting mode...  High dexterity helps, but it is still very
difficult to tackle an opponent even if your dexterity is high.  If you
fail the tackle, you will be off-balance for the next 3-4 rounds, so if
you are planning on fleeing soon, it is not wise to tackle.


SEE ALSO: GROUNDFIGHTING

0 CIRCLE~
{W}Circle
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{N}Level : {W}28
{N}Preqs : {p}Piercing Weapons, Backstab
{N}Guilds: {C}Thief, Marauder
{N}
Syntax: Circle

This skill allows you to sneak around an opponent and place a suitable
piercing weapon in his/her/its back during combat.  Your target must be
fighting someone else (IE you must be assisting someone else).

A word of caution: often the opponent will get angry and turn and attack
you after a successful circle.

Just like Backstab a Thief will circle for a greater ammount then a
Marauder because Marauders spent time learning warrior skills along
with learning their thief skills.

SEE ALSO: BACKSTAB
          FLASH
          DUAL DAGGERS
          DUAL BACKSTAB

{R}NOTE: Must have flash powder in your hands to use this skill!{N}

Flash lets you get in an "instant circle". In order to use it, you must
be wielding a dagger in one hand, and holding flash powder in the other.
Then type "flash" once you are already engaged and you will attempt
to get in an instant circle (Even if your opponent is attacking you!).
Flash powder is rare, so save this for important fights.

0 ARMORCLASS AC 'ARMOR CLASS'~
Armors like breastplates, helmets and various protective spells can
all be used to lower your "Armor" value.  The more armored you are,
the more damage can be "absorbed" from an attack.  If you are well-
enough armored, many attacks will not even reach your skin, and will
just give you a small bruise.  Armor is not a 100% surefire way to
stop all attacks, though; often an opponent will be able to find an
opening on even a person with incredible armor and the armor may absorb
little or none of the blow.
~

0 STUDY~
Syntax: Study <object>

This command will allow you to study a book, manuscript or text.  If the
book/etc.. contains useful information about a spell or a skill, you will
be able to learn about the spell or skill inscribed upon the text.
Reading a book that shows you what you already know will not improve your
proficiency in that skill.
~

feline      plant     dummy *****

** Note: Ghosts can only be hit by glowing or humming weapons
*** Werebeasts are mobs that will change from one mob to another at
    10 pm and 5 am.
**** Nightbeasts are beasts that go to sleep when sun comes out or they
     get hurt.  I.e. Vampires.
***** Dummy mobs will not fight back.  Do not even think of having dummy
      mobs without asking a god first.
If you think something should be changed or added, let me know.  Remember,
ALL mobs should have a mobtype set.

101 'IREF FURNITURE' FURNITURE~
As of the creation of this help file, there is only enterable furniture.
This is made by setting obj-type to furniture, and setting the proper
values.  v0 = 4, and v1 = the destination room vnum.  For example, if
v1 = 00, then entering the object would take you to room #00.
Make sure you don't make enterable objects takable, or people have an
infinite # of teleports!

109 SEDIT~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                           {R}   SEDIT LEVEL 111
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

These are the damage and duration spell variables to construct a
formula.  The rest is self explanitory.


   a                  = random from 1-10
   b                  = random from 10-20
   c                  = random from 20-30
   d                  = random from 12-48 For Durations
   e                  = Elemental's Guild 1, else 0
   f                  = Thief's Guild then 1, else 0
   g                  = Wizard's Guild then 1, else 0
   h                  = Healer's Guild then 1, else 0
   i                  = char's intelligence
   j                  = Battlemage's Guild then 1, else 0
   k                  = kick damage
   l                  = level
   m                  = Syntax m42 would be max of 42 damage (numeric only)
   n                  = Necromancer's Guild
   o                  = Warrior's Guild then 1, else 0
   p                  = Paladin's Guild then 1, else 0
   q		      = OPEN
   r		      = Plus Magic Damage
   s                  = char's strength
   t                  = Max Hit Do not know what this is... do not use it.
   u                  = Marauder's Guild then 1, else 0
   v                  = Heal Bonus for Plus Heal eq
   w                  = char's wisdom
   x                  = char's con
   y                  = char's dex
   z                  = Syntax z3 would be minimum 3 damage (numeric only)

please note: all operations are performed from left to right.  This makes
for simple coding, and a damn quick pass thru a complicated expression.

sample:

  l+w/3        would be written in real terms as: l/3 + w/3 or (l+w)/3
  i+w+l*2/3+l  would be written in real terms as: (((i+w)+l)*2)/3)+l
  25*h+b       would be 25 damage if in healer's guild, plus random from 10-20

{C}This is to set guild requirements on spells.
{N}Sedit Guild flags:
Syntax:
guild1 <flag name> guild2 <flag name> guild3 <flag name>

{G}warriorg   = Warrior guild
rangerg    = Ranger guild
assassing  = Assassin guild
thiefg     = Thief guild
palading   = Paladin guild
elementg   = Elemental guild
battleg    = Battlemage guild
marauderg  = Marauder guild
necrog     = Necromancer guild


{B}Commands within the spell editor:

{N}DONE 		Exits the spell editor.
NAME <name>	Sets the spell's name.  This name is the name of the spell. 
		Do not change the name of skills, or there will be internal
		problems with lookups.
NAME2 <name>	Sets the spell's name.  This was used in the past, but it
		should be the same as the NAME field now.
NDAM <word>	If the spell is offensive, this is the word that is
		places in combat text.  Example: NDAM fireball
		Shows: Joe's fireball MANGLES you! or......
		Joe fireballs you very hard.
DAMG <string>	See above for variables.  This sets the damage the spell
		does.  (Unless heals_dams is set, in which case this is
		the amount of healing, or if add_moves is set, this is the
		 move gain).
WEAR_OFF <text>	This is the wear-off message for spells that have duration.
		For instance:  You feel weaker..might be a message for
		a strength spell wear_off.
DURATION <str>	This can contain variables (see above).  This is used 
		to set the duration of a spell if the spell is one that 
		lasts.  (IE strength spell).
PRE1 <name>	SEts the firest prerequisite to the spell.  Can be blank.
		The character must be proficient in this specified skill
		or spell in order to learn this skill/spell.  Example:
		editing backstab, I might have PRE1 PIERCING to make
		piercing weapons a prerequisite to backstab.
PRE2 <name>	This sets the second prerequisite.  See above.
MODIFIER <str>	This string con contain variables and tells how MUCH the
		spell will modify something.  For instance, a weaken spell
		might have a modifier of -2, or (1/25)m3
MWIS <wis>	For spells only, this sets the minimum wisdom required to
		understand this spell.  If the character trying to learn the
		spell's wisdom is lower, they cannot learn it as well.
MINT <int>	For spells only, see above, but with intelligence.
MCON <con>	For skills only, see above, but with constitution.
MSTR <str>	For skills only, see above, but with strength.
MANA <amount>	How much mana this spell takes at minimum.
LVL <level>	The level at which a character can learn this spell/skill if
		he/she finds the practitioner.
TIME <time>  	This sets the casting time for the spell.  Experiment around
		with holylag on to determine the correct time.  8 is almost
		equal to one "combat" round.
DELAY <time>	Same as above, just another word to modify the same field.
CREATES_OBJ <vnum>	This specifies if the spell is to create an object.
			when cast.  This can be used in conjunction with
			flags to make the object appear in the room as well.
			This is used for create food/create spring/etc spells.
STANDING	Specifies the player must be in standing position to 
		cast the spell.  (IE can't be fighting).
RESTING		Unused.  Should be standing or fighting.
FIGHTING	Specifies the player can be either fighting or standing
		to cast the spell.  (IE the spell is castable in combat).
FIRE		These mana types specify which mana type the spell requires.
AIR		If you specify more than one, it will work, but the mana
EARTH		type displayed on slist/spells will not be correct, so it
WATER		is recommended you use only one.
DEATH		Specifies ANY mana type can be used for this spell.
ANY

For modifiers, you can use any of those mentioned above in the object section
under addaffect.  IE" strength, intelligence, dexterity, armor, etc...

For bits, you can use any of the bits mentioned above under the GENERAL
AFFECTS FLAG section in mob editing.  IE:  APOISON, SANCTUARY,
PLAGUE, etc...

The target field of a spell
The spell must know what sort of target it is looking for...

OFFENSIVE	This requires a player/mob name if not fighting, or if fighting, it defaults
		to your opponent.  It initiates combat if cast upon a player/mob.  Spells
		such as 'magic missile', 'weaken', and 'plague' fall into this category.
DEFENSIVE	This accepts a player/mob name, or if none is given, the default is for the 
		spell to be cast on the caster.  Spells such as 'shield' and 'strength' fall
		into this category.
SELF		This spell can only be cast ont he caster (self).  It cannot be cast on 
		anybody else.
NONE		(aka IGNORE).  This spell target is used for things such as create object
		spells, etc, where you cannot cast the spell on anybody or yourself.
OBJINV		This requires the caster to specify an object in inventory.  For spells like
		identify.

Special BITS that allow cool spells

SUMMON		This spell behaves like a summon spell.
		SPECS:  Cannot summon someone > 5 levels above you.
		Cannot summon mobs unless specified on it power.dat
		Cannot summon someone from a room with vnum < 1000.
		Cannot summon fighting character/mobs.
		Cannot summon from/to nosummon rooms.
		Cannot summon cross-alignment.
TELEPORT	This spell behaves like the teleport spell.
		SPECS:  Destination rooms is from 1001 to 99999.
		Will choose a room in an open area, not in a swim 
		or no-swim room.
		WARNING:  If you have no rooms above 1001 that aren't
		in an open area or are all swim and no-swim the mud will
		go into a repeating loop here, trying to find an acceptable
		room to teleport into.  Since it will never find one, you
		must kill the mud process to stop the repeating loop.
ALL_IN_ROOM	This bit specifies that the spells should affect everyboby
		in the room of the caster.  Can be used in conjunction with
		other flags!  (see below)
ONLY_MULTI_MOBS	This flag specifies than an ALL_IN_ROOM flagged spell will
		only affect multiple mobs, and not multiple players.
		This can be used for an ice shards spell, for instance, where
		you want it to hit multiple mobs, but when used against
		other players, only to hit one player (the target).
ONLY_GROUP	This flag specifies that an ALL_IN_ROOM flagged spell will 
		only affect people of the casters same general alignment.
		(ie: evil/evil, good/good, not evil/good or good/evil).
		This can be used for a mass heal spell, for instance.
ONLY_NOT_GROUP	This flag specifies that an ALL_IN_ROOM flagged spell will 
		only affect people of an opposing group (evil/good, good/evil)
		This can be used for fireballs pell, for instance.
REMOVES_BIT	Instead of adding the specified bit (see above) to the
		victim(s), it removes the bit.  Used for cure blindness,
		cure poison, cure plague, etc...
HEALS_DAM	Used for healing spells.  Instead of doing the damage 
		specified in the DAM field, this will heal that specified
		amount of damage.
MESSAGE		This is the message spell.  Usage:
		cast 'message' joe Hello joe, how are you!
		This can be used cross-alignment.  Many admin opt not to 
		make a spell that uses this, as it can be abused.
DISPEL_MAGIC	This spell removes a random affect from the target(s).
		Fails if the victim makes one of two saving rolls.
		Fails if the victim is over 30 levels above the caster.
HURT_EVIL	This spell only will affect evil players (ie dispel evil)
HURT_GOOD	This spell only will affect good/neutral players.
		Note this could be used for defensive spells as well, not
		only dispel good/etc...
HURT_UNDEAD	This spell only affects undead creatures (ghosts, undead).
IDENTIFY	This is the identify spell if this flag is on.

SCRY		This is the scry spell (shows the room and contents of the
		room the victim is in).  SPECS:
		Fails if victim is hidden. (even if caster has detect hidden)
		Fails if victim is in a no-track room.
		Fails if victim is greater than 17 levels than caster.
		Fails if victim cannot be seen by the caster (ie invis, and 
		caster doesn't have detect invis).
LOCATE_PERSON	This is the locate person spell (it shows the room NAME
		that the victim is in).  SPECS:
		Same as scry, except restricted to 10 level difference
		between caster and victim
RECALL		The recall spell...takes the victim back to their 
		respective recall location. SPECS:
		Fails if caster is in a no-recall room.
		Fails if the caster is fighting.
		Fails if cast upon an oppositely aligned player.
FAIL1/2		This spell fails 1/2 of the time.
FAIL1/3		This spell fails 1/3 of the time.
FAIL1/4		This spell fails 1/4 of the time.
		Can be used together with cumulative effect.
ACID		Randomly dissolves equipment on the victim. SPECS:
		Dissolves no equipment if (2*(caster level)) is lower
		than a random number between 1 and 120.
		56% chance of hitting an object, less if you are 
		wearing almost no armor.
		Removes 3 "hit" points from armor if armor is hit.
		Dissolves container and all contents if a container
		is hit (backpack, etc).
FIREFLAG	Random burns equipment on the victim.  SPECS:
		Burns no equipment if (2*(caster level)) is lower than
		a random number between 1 and 100 or if the victim makes
		a saving throw.  Burns only 10 percent of objects, but will
		burn containers, potions, scrolls, staffs, wands, food, and
		pills.
TWO_SAVES	Gives the victim two saves to resist the effects if this
		is a spell like weaken, etc...
DAM1/2		Halves the damage of offensive spells if the victim makes
		a saving throw.
NOT_SELF	Specifies this spell CANNOT be cast on yourself (the caster).
		Please note the opposite of this is a SELF target spell.
OBJ_TO_ROOM	Specifies that the creates_obj <vnum> object will go to 
		the room instead of the character.
ADD_MOVE	Specifies that instead of using the damage field to calculate
		damage, it will be used to calculate how many moves to add
		on to the victim(s).  Used for refresh/mass refresh spells, etc.

Spell cast messages

Spell cast messages use the following variables:

$N (substitutes the name of the VICTIM.. the person upon whom the spell is being cast).
$n (substitutes the name of the PERSON...the caster).
$M (substitutes him/her/it for the VICTIM)
$m (substitutes him/her/it for the CASTER)
$S (substitutes he/she/it for the VICTIM)
$s (substitutes he/she/it for the CASTER)

TO_CHAR1 <string>	This is shown to the character casting the spell.
TO_CHAR2 <string>	This is also shown to the character casting the spell.
			Example: You heal $N!
			or.....Your strength spell was a success....
TO_VICT1 <string>	This is shown to the victim of the spell, or
TO_VICT2 <string>	whom you are casting it upon.
			Example: $n heals you!
			or...You feel stronger!
TO_NOTVICT1 <string>	This is shown to the peope in the room who aren't
TO_NOTVICT1 <string>	the caster or the victim.
			Example: $n heals $N!
			or......$N's muscles bulge with increased power!

LINK <snum>	This command can be used to link a spell with another spell
		number.  For instance, if I want a spell to damage a victim
		and also heal the caster, I would have my damage spell LINK
		to the number of my heal spell.  Thus, heal would be cast
		every time this damage spell is cast....you get the idea :)
~

0 LINKLESS 'BAD LINK'~
Just so we don't get any complaints, we will warn you now:  Linkless
characters are VERY vunerable and can be taken advantage of easily!  If
you are being hunted by orcs, you cannot simply drop link; you will
remain linkless and they will be able to hit/attack you.  You will,
however flee when you become linkless and get attacked.  This prevents
cheating (being hunted or dropping link near death).  If you drop link
and die; TOUGH LUCK!  Wine, complain if you wish, but we warned you and
you will recieve NO help or reimbursement whatsoever.

The policy is simple: If you drop link and die; too bad.  We're truly
sorry for you, but no action will be taken.
~

0 CRASHES CRASH~
Crashes happen occasionally (about once every 5-8 hours at the moment).
Save every 3-5 minutes or after you kill a big mob or do a trade.
Be assured that when you die, your corpse is saved to disk and even
if a crash occurs your corpse will still be where you died.

NO REIMBURSEMENTS WILL BE GIVEN FOR CRASHES AT BAD TIMES!  PERIOD.
~

103 reset~
{B}{B}[{G}+{B}]-=-=--=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=--=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{B}[{G}+{B}]
                                {R}RESET
{B}{B}[{G}+{B}]-=-=--=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=--=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{B}[{G}+{B}]

This is the help file for setting resets in rooms for mobs and objects.
I will try and make this as simple as possible but if you have any question
on setting resets do not be afraid to ask.

MOB Syntax: reset <reset #> mob <mob vnum> <% mob repops> <number in room>
OBJ Syntax: reset <reset #> obj <obj vnum> <location> <% obj repops on mob>

Make it easy on yourself and make all mobs reset at 100% and load only
1 mob in a room of that kind.

Ok when you create a mob you will need to reset the mob in a room so it
will repop when the area repops. If you are going to load an item in a room
like as in a fountain, a box, or a portal the resets are just a bit different.

For and item in a room like a fountain:
reset 1 obj <vnum of fountain or other object> room <% of items load>

To load a weapon, armor, key, gem on a mob you must make sure the mobs reset
number is before the objects reset number

If you type:

reset 2 mob 4432 100 1

it should look like this when done

{G}2{g} - {g}Loads a {G}golden statue of Razlin {g}({C}4432{g}) in room (max {G}1 {g}at {G}100%{g} chance

Reason it is reset 2 is because there is a portal loading in the room first which is setup like this:

reset 1 obj 4378 room 100

Should look like this when you type reset:

{G}1{g}-  Loads {B}b{b}l{B}u{b}e {W}glowing {g}portal ({G}4378{g}) in room {R}100%{g} chance

There is also an item loading on the mob to reset that would be:

reset 3 obj 4432 none 100

Should look like this when you type reset:

{G}3{g}-  Loads a {Y}b{y}r{Y}a{y}c{Y}e{y}r{g} of the {B}g{b}o{B}d{b}s {g}({G}4432{g}) on {C}none {g}of {G}a golden statue of Razlin 
{R}5% {g}chance

So when you type reset in the room you would see a total of three resets looking like this:

{G}1{g}-  Loads {B}b{b}l{B}u{b}e {W}glowing {g}portal ({G}4378{g}) in room {R}100%{g} chance{G}
{G}2{g} - Loads a {G}golden statue of Razlin {g}({C}4432{g}) in room (max {G}1 {g}at {G}100%{g} chance
{G}3{g}-  Loads a {Y}b{y}r{Y}a{y}c{Y}e{y}r{g} of the {B}g{b}o{B}d{b}s {g}({G}4432{g}) on {C}none {g}of {G}a golden statue of Razlin
{R}5% {g}chance


This is a list of <location> keywords for the RESET command for objects.

lfinger         shield
rfinger         about                     You may sheath 2 weapons
neck1           waist                 |-------------------------------|
neck2           lwrist                     belt1            belt2
body            rwrist                            (weapon)

hold1           hold2
ear1            ear2
ankle1          ankle2
inside - Will load inside of a box or bag if item is container.
room - load the item in the room (like a fountain)

Any questions about resets ask.

much.

0 MOVEMENT 'MOVEMENT COMMANDS'~
N, S, E, W, Up, Down move you in the direction if you can go that way.

RUN: Run's syntax is RUN <direction> <number of squares>.  You may often run
     past aggressive mobs, although many guarding mobs will not let you by.
     Run will get you past players spamming "kill xxxx" and also allow you
     to avoid tintin autohunt.

CLIMB: Syntax is CLIMB <up/down> <object name>.  For instance, Climb up tree.

ENTER: Syntax is ENTER <object/thing in room>.  For instance, enter portal.

TRACK: Syntax is TRACK <player>.  Depends on membership in Ranger's Guild or
       how well you know the track skill.
~

0 ATTRIBUTE ATT~
This command shows a bit about your character: his/her stats and fight
information, as well as total kills and kill points.  Typing att or
attribute will display the information.

Also type either: SCORE or INFO
~

0 STATS STRENGTH CONSTITUTION WISDOM INTELLIGENCE DEXTERITY~
Strength:     This stat speaks for itself.
              What it affects:
              Your carrying capacity and extra damage you do in battle,
              How well you can resist disarms in combat, how well you can
              bash down doors, etc...

Constitution: This stat is your health or well being.
              What it affects:
              How many hitpoints you get after a level, and other smaller
              aspects related to your "toughness".

Wisdom:       This stat shows how wise you are.
              What it affects:
              How many practices you gain after you level, and your
              natural mana and maximum mana with gems.

Intelligence: This stat shows how intelligent you are.
              What it affects:
              How fast you learn new spells.  It also helps in casting
              offense spells and affects natural mana.

Dexterity:    This stat shows how agile and quick you are.
              What it affects:
              How well you move during battle, dodge trips, and how fast you
              gain back lost movement points.
~

0 CLANTALK~
Syntax: clantalk <message>

This is just like any other communication channel, except this one only
transmits to your clan only.

See Also: CLAN, CLANS, GUILD
~

0 POSITION 'POSITION COMMANDS'~
FLY   will make you fly if you are a dragonkin or have cast the FLY spell.
LAND  will make you land if you are flying.
REST  will make you rest.  You can see people come/go but you don't get
      hit points or movement back as fast as if you were sleeping.
SLEEP puts your character to sleep, allowing him/her to regenerate.
STAND makes your character stand (and wake if you are sleeping).
WAKE  makes your character wake and stand if you are asleep.
SNEAK is based on how well you have practiced sneak, and will allow you
      to move between rooms undetected.
HIDE  allows you to hide in a room, possibly undetected until you type
      a command or move.

MEDITATE  allows you to regenerate mana at a faster rate.
SURRENDER allows you to go to jail if you are an outlaw and a guard is in
          the room.  See help surrender.
SEARCH    allows you to search the room for hidden objects, or a direction
          for a hidden door.
MOUNT     is the same as Ride.  Syntax is Ride/Mount <Mobile to ride>.
DISMOUNT  is the command to get off the ridden mobile.
VISIBLE   will remove invisibility, sneak, and hide, making you visible.

~

0 GUILDS GUILD~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                                       GUILDS
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
NOTE: GUILDMASTERS and PRACTITIONERS are NOT the same!  You cannot join
for instance, the warrior's guild at the WARRIOR practitioner!

If you've never taken a history class or have forgotten:  Guilds are
groups of skilled laborers/professionals that get together and basically
form a monopoly on the business/skill level.  Guilds are not secret,
tightly knit groups (see CLANS), but they are just members of people who
share common interests.  

{B}The guilds currently in the lands are:

{R}Main Guilds
{C}Thief's Guild, 
Warrior's Guild, 
Healer's Guild,
Wizard's Guild, 
Elemental Guild, 
Marauder's Guild,
Battlemage's Guild, 
Paladin Guild, {R}Not all spells complete atm{C}
Necromancer Guild, {R}Some spells done already: All Animate spells in{C}

{R}Secondary Guilds
{C}Assassin's Guild,
Tinker's Guild,
Ranger's Guild,
Shaman's Guild,
Mystic's Guild,
Tactic's Guild
{N}

Guild Combos

{R}Single Class Guilds
{W}Warrior's Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild, {R}Tactic's Guild.
{B}Elemental Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild, {b}Mystic's Guild.
{R}Wizard's Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild, {b}Mystic's Guild.
{P}Thief's Guild, {G}Assassin's Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild.
{Y}Healer's Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild, {y}Shaman's Guild.
{d}Necromancer Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {b}Mystic's Guild, {y}Shaman's Guild.

{R}Dual Class Guilds
{C}Paladin Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild, {y}Shaman's Guild.
{P}Marauder's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {R}Tactic's Guild.
{B}Battlemage's Guild, {g}Ranger's Guild, {c}Tinker's Guild, {R}Tactic's Guild.

{N}
You can find help on each guild by typing HELP <guildname> like HELP WARRIOR.  
When you join a guild, you gain certain advantages depending on what the guild
specializes in.  For instance, tinkers pay less to repair goods, clerics'
guildmembers' spells are more powerful than those not in the guild,
warriors fight a little bit better, etc...  Guild members can be total
enemies, good friends or total strangers; it doesn't matter.  If you are
in a guild, it simply means you are a specialist in the guild's area (and
have gone through their training program).  When you join a guild, you
will go through an instantaneous training program that enhances your
skills, depending on the guild.  SEE ALSO:  Help CLANS

PLEASE NOTE: Some guilds don't get along with eachother... ask around
before you go joining a guild, and plan ahead.

0 CLANS~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{c}Clans are tightly-woven social groups that stick together through thick
and thin.  A clan usually has a leader, which can organize meetings,
broadcast messages to fellow clan-members and organize raids/hunting
parties.  Being in a clan has no statistical advantages to your
character, although clan-members generally look after one another.  Once
you are in a clan, you are a member until kicked out by vote or you
switch alignments and the clan does not approve.  Each clan has their own
special channel for communication, and a notify beeper.  A notify message
appears whenever a clan-member raises a level, gets killed, or kills
another player.  For all you college people: a clan is like being in a
fraternity or sorority.  For info on the clan you are in (if any) type {R}CLAN

{N}If you are a clanleader, please see {R}HELP CLEADER
{N}If you are interested in starting a CLAN, see help {R}STARTCLAN
{N}For info on buying guards, building rooms for your clan, type help {R}CBUILD
{B}SEE ALSO: {R}HELP GUILDS{N}
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 CLEADER~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
As a clanleader, you have access to three extra commands:

CADD <name> will add a character to the clan.  The character need not be
            playing at the time he/she is added.  The clan will be notified
            when a new member is added.

CREMOVE <name> will remove a character from the clan.  The character need
            not be playing at the time he/she is removed.

ANNOUNCE <string> will send an announcement via CLAN Notify to all
            members of the clan currently online.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 ALIAS ALIASES MACRO MACROS~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: alias      (shows your current aliases)
Syntax: alias <characters> <does-this>
Syntax: alias <name of alias>     (deletes the alias)

A '*' character in an alias will be considered as if you pressed enter.

Example: alias 5 sleep       -will make you sleep after you type: 5  <enter>
Example: alias rs rest       -will make you rest after you  type: rs <enter>
Example: alias yum get bread*eat bread*smile
Example: alias k kill

Aliases are used so you don't have to type so much.  It also enables you
to do multiple tasks such as: backstab, flee, run south.

-Note: if you give an argument to the alias, it will use it as an argument
       to the last command in the alias.  (i.e., using the 'k'='kill'
       example, 'k bear' will come out as 'kill bear'.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 BREAK~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: Break [dir or doorname]

BREAK will allow a player to try and break a door.  If you look at the
direction you want to break in, it'll tell you how strong the door is.
If the door breaks open, it'll close on reset.  If it's broken, it
is broken for good.  Or at least until the next reboot.

0 FLURRY~

Flurry is a combat skill that allows you to flail about madly in a
wild flurry.  Because of the extreme energies required to go berserk
like this, you will end up losing many stamina points.  So...  if you are
planning to run after the battle, this is not a good option.  Anyone can
flurry with or without a weapon.

0 GROUNDFIGHT GROUNDFIGHTING 'GROUND FIGHTING'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
The mud will not let you groundfight before level 11 or 12, due to the
huge loss of hit points.  It is also recommended that you configure the
groundfighting option OFF.  (Type FIGHT to see your combat options)

Ocassionally in battle, the fighters will miss a bash and trip, or one
will tackle another.  The fight will be then taken to the ground.
Ground-fighting is no-nonsense and fast; close in biting and headbutting
can kill in extremely short amounts of time.  Once you are on the ground,
you perform on instinct.  Hard helmets make head-butts harder, masks can
protect against elbows to the face, and many other factors can
increase/decrease damage taken.

    If you are fighting multiple opponents, it will become difficult for
them to find a line of attack (since you are twisted up on the ground with
your opponent...)  However, if another attacker does find a line of
attack, he/she/it can slash/pierce/whatever you.  Since you are entangled
with your opponent, you will not be able to dodge or parry the incoming
attacks.  Also, a person assisting a groundfighting player/mob without a
weapon will not punch anymore; he/she/it will now stomp.  Stomps also
usually do more damage.  In general, it is not recommended that you go to
the ground with multiple oponents.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 MEDITATE MEDITATION~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: Meditate

This command allows you to sit down and meditate, allowing the gem in
your hand to charge at a greatly increased rate.  You will, however, not
receive the massive bonuses to move and hit points that you might receive
if you slept or rested.  Typing meditate while already meditating will stop
you meditating and bring you to your feet.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 EXCHANGE SWAP~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: Exchange
Syntax: Swap

This command switches items in your primary and secondary hands.  If two
items are held, the positions exchange.  If one item is help, its position
switches between primary and secondary hand.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

0 GLANCE~

0 SPAM NOSPAM~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: nospam
Syntax: spam

This command is essential in large groups with anything slower than a 56k
link.  Nospam mode only shows the hits that take place during combat,
and later, will cut down the general spam associated with groups.
To bring back SPAM mode, type spam.  There are THREE levels of spam.
FULL, MODERATE and NOSPAM.  Use spam command to toggle between them.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 ANSI COLOR~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: ansi toggle
Syntax: ansi <channel> <color name>
Syntax: ansi <channel> <color index number>
Syntax: config +ansi

For those of you with terminals which support ANSI Color codes, the 'ANSI'
command can be used to configure ansi for your system.

To change colors of channels (only global channels) type ansi <channel> <color code from help title>

Example: ansi chat $B$4 would make chat look like this.
{B}You Chat, Hi{g}

TELL = Can not change this channel
GOSSIP = Same as Chat level 15+
CLANTALK = Clan channel only
AUCTION
YELL = Can not change this channel
NEWBIE = level 1-15 chat
