110 hedit~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                   Hedit
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
 
ONE AT A TIME IN HEDIT - or guess what :) mud goes poofy!!
 
rld_help is only used if you edit a help file from shell
if you use rld_help you will lose all help files you have made.
 
Hedit:
 
Hedit <keyword> - lets you edit a help file already made.
 
Hedit create <keyword> - creates a new help file.
 
Ok while in hedit:
 
Edit: - lets you edit the help file you are in - just like note
 
level <number> - Sets the level of who can see the help file.
 
done - quits and saves the help file.
 
Code added by Geist and Odie 6/5/2000
~

110 battle ground setup~
Ok to start a battle ground it is:
 
setlevel [level] [level] [prize vnum] [prize vnum]
 
IE: setlevel 1 90 1001 2345
 
Them prize vnums are made up so if there is not an item for them please
dont use it because they wont work :)
~

110 spell_flags spell-flags~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                     Spell Flags
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
 
These are the special bits used on spells.
 
Summon - This spell behaves like a summon spell.
Teleport - This behaves like the teleport spell.
all_in_room - This means the spell will affect everybody in the room of the caster.
only_multi_mobs - This will only affect all the mobs in a room.
only_group - this means an all_in_room flag will only affect people in the spell
            casters group.
only_not_group - This means that the all_in_room flag will affect everyone 
               NOT in the group of the caster.
removes_bit - this is used for spells like cure blindness.
heals_dam - Used for healing spells.
message - DO NOT USE!!
dispel_magic - this flag removes a random affect from the target of the spell.
hurt_evil - this spell only affects those with evil alignment.
hurt_good - Affects only those with netural/good alignments.
hurt_undead - hurts only undead creatures (ghosts, undead)
scry - This is the scry spell, shows the room and contents of the target of the spell.
locate_person - it shows the name of the room the target is in.
recall - this is the recall spell.
fail1/2 - makes spell fail 1/2 of the time.
fail1/3 - makes spell fail 1/3 of the time.
fail1/4 - makes spell fail 1/4 of the time.
acid - randomly dissolves eq on the victim.
fireflag - randomly burns eq on the victim.
two_saves - gives the victim two saves to resist the effects of this spell like weaken.
dam1/2 - halves the damage of offensive spells if the victim makes a saving throw.
not_self means spell cannot be casted on the caster.
obj_to_room - specifies that creates_obj <vnum> obj goes to room and not character.
add_move - this is used for the refresh spell.
~

110 pedit~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                   {R}Pedit
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Height - sets players height in inches. 
Name - Sets a players name.
Race <number. - this sets a players race. 0 = Human.
Sex <number> - sets players sex 0=nuter 1=male 2=female.
remort <number> - sets a persons ammount of remorts *dont play with this*
email <email addy> - sets a persons email addy.
nat <number> - sets players natural armor class.
death <number> - sets persons ammount of deaths.
war <number> - sets players warpoints *do not play with*
room <vnum> - will set where the player will log in at.
bank <number> - sets the player's bank in copper.
Prac <number> - sets player's practices.
Learns <number> - same as prac but for learns.
hpnow <number> - sets ammount of players hp now 234<-amm now/300hp
hp <number> - sets max ammount of hp.

~

0 replace~
Syntax: Replace learns - to receive 10 practice sessions.

Syntax: Replace practices - to receive 1 learn session.
 
The replace command is to fluidly switch around practices and learns in order
to make it easier for the player to learn skills/spells without having to wait
for a level.
 
NOTE: This command can only be used when the user reached level 10.
~

0 'ROLLING COMBOS' rolling~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                ROLLING COMBOS FOR CLASSES
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Ok this to help get a good roll with your character.

Warrior Classes try: ABEA
Thief Classes   try: FEBE
Mage Classes    try: BCDB
Healer Classes  try: CDCF
Paladin         try: EAFD

If you want to take the chance and get an over all roll (best with humans)
try: DFAC

Or you can try all the different combos and see if you can come up with something better :)
Good luck and have fun

                        Skill and Spell practice levels
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

This help file will show you the range of what percent your skill
or spell is at when you see the names beside them.

-100% - 1%  unlearned
0% ---- 4%  beginner
5% ---- 9%  poor
10% -- 14%  novice
15% -- 19%  moderate
20% -- 29%  good
30% -- 39%  skilled
40% -- 49%  adept
50% -- 59%  talented
60% -- 69%  gifted
70% -- 79%  Superb
80% -- 89%  MasteR
90% -- 95%  PerFecT
96% - 100%  GODLY

0 'eqlist'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                    {R}EqList
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax config eqlist.

This is a config option for your eqlist.

If you type config eqlist it will change the way your eq command shows
what you are wearing.

Standard eqlist
You are using:
 Nothing.

config eqlist style 1
All equipment slots will be shown.

You are using:
<worn on finger>    nothing
<worn on finger>    nothing
<worn around neck>  nothing
<worn around neck>  nothing
<worn on body>      nothing
all eq slots this is just a small example

config eqlist style 2
Equipment will be sorted from head to toe, empty slots will not be shown.

If you are wearing eq it will show the eq you are wearing from your head
to your toes starting with:
<floating nearby>  to <worn on feet>
Empty eq slots will not be shown

config eqlist style 3
Equipment will be sorted from head to toe, all slots will be shown.

This is just like the style above showing your eq from
<floating nearby>  to <worn on feet>
and also showing slots where you have no eq as

<floating nearby>   nothing
<floating nearby>   nothing
<worn on head>      nothing
<worn in ear>       nothing
<worn in ear>       nothing
<worn on left eye>  nothing
<worn on face>      nothing
<worn around neck>  nothing
<worn around neck>  nothing
<worn about body>   nothing

{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

103 'ADDAFFECTS' 'removeaffect'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                                  ADDAFFECT & REMAFFECT
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

Syntax: addaffect <what-affect-added> <modifier #> <1>
Syntax: remaffect <what-affect-added>

ADDAFFECT <location> <amount> 1   For this command it gets a little more detailed.

Addaffect adds an affect to the object. For instance, if you want an object
that takes away 2 strength from the wearer, you would use the command:

Addaffect strength -2 1

Here is a list of all the affects you can add to items in the game and the limits allowed.

{R}STATS:
{R}str {N}- {R}ASK TO ADD TO ANY ITEM!
{R}int {N}- {R}ASK TO ADD TO ANY ITEM!
{R}dex {N}- {R}ASK TO ADD TO ANY ITEM!
{R}con {N}- {R}ASK TO ADD TO ANY ITEM!
{R}wis {N}- {R}ASK TO ADD TO ANY ITEM!

{N}OTHER AFFECTS:
hp {N}............... on a single location item max of +25 on a double location item max of +10
move {N}............. on a single location item max of +25 on a double location item max of +10

{R}*NOTE* on AC and SAVING_THROW negitive (-) is good and positive (+) is bad.
{B}ac {N}............... on a single location item max of -3 on a double location item max of -1
{B}hit {N}.............. on a single location item max of +5 on a double location item max of +2
{B}dam {N}.............. on a single location item max of +1 on a double location item max of +1
{B}saving_throw {N}..... on a single location item max of -3 on a double location item max of -1
{B}resist_summon {N}.... on a single location item max of -3 on a double location item max of -1

{R}*NOTE* Plus kick can only be put on items legs, knee, feet, ankle.
{B}kick_dam {N}......... on a single location item max of +4 on a double location item max of +3
{B}hide_bonus {N}....... on a single location item max of +5 on a double location item max of +3
{B}bs_dam {N}........... on a single location item max of +5 on a double location item max of +3
{B}sneak_bonus {N}...... on a single location item max of +5 on a double location item max of +3
{B}magic_dam {N}........ on a single location item max of +5 on a double location item max of +3
{B}heal_bonus {N}....... on a single location item max of +5 on a double location item max of +3

Make sure you add the addaffect in the name of the item.

example of an item:
 a {d}black {N}stone anklet

{g}Syntax: name anklet stone black ankle +3 KICK


{R}ALSO SEE: OEDIT, WEAPONS, WEAR-LOCATIONS
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

103 'WEAR-LOCATIONS'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
                             WEAR-LOCATIONS
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}

in the name field of the object.

example of an item:
 a {d}black {N}stone anklet

{g}Syntax: name anklet stone black ankle +3 KICK

{R}take {N}... Make sure all items have take on them if the player is to be able to use them.

0 'DARKIE' 'WHITIE' 'DARKIES' 'WHITIES'~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                        WHITIES AND DARKIES
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
This help file is to explain Whities and Darkies. All whities and darkies
stand for is good and evil. They are names that have been with EmlenMud
for a long time and kind of sets this apart from the other type of MU*s
out in the world.

If you are a Darkie you are Evil and your home town is Masqe. {R}See HELP MASQE{N}
If you are a Whitie you are Good and your home town is Xylar. {B}See HELP XYLAR{N}

Also see:
{r}HELP NEWBIE
HELP MUDMAP
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 implant implants~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                           Implants
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Implants help you in different ways. below is a list of implants and
the bonuses they give to you. You must find the operating room and
have enough hitpoints, movement points, warpoints, experience,
warpoints, and gold needed to recieve the following implants.

Arm strength implant   - This implant helps with inflicting melee damage to others.
                         Also helps to inflict more damage in ground fights.
Leg strength implant   - This implant helps to inflict more damage with kick.
Hand strength implant  - This like Arm strength helps inflict more melee damage.
                         Also helps to inflict more damage in ground fights.
Body strength implant  - This also helps in melee damage.
		  	 Also helps to inflict more damage in ground fights.
Arm dexterity implant  - This implant helps inflict more backstab and circle damage.
Leg durability implant - Helps while over weight in preventing movement loss.
Arcane implant         - This helps in inflicting more offensive magical damage and also
                         helps to asorb more damage while trying to cast.
Metal feet implant     - Helps in inflicting more kick damage and also adds a bit
                         armor to your legs.
Metal hand implant     - Adds more armor to your arms.
Steel armor implant    - Adds more armor to your body.

The implants you have will show up with the armor command.
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 STORE STORAGE~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                                Bank Storage
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
There are a few commands you can do at the bank to store items.

At any time you can type store to get a list of what items you own that
are stored in your bank storage. You can ONLY take them out of the bank
when you are at a bank teller.

syntax: store <item>
Will tell you how much it will cost to take that item out of the bank
later.

syntax: store <item> yes
Will store the item in the bank (if it is storable.)

To remove an item from the bank:

First of all you must have enough money either in your bank account or 
on your person to remove the item.

syntax: unstore <item> or <number>
Will list how much the item will cost to unstore.

syntax: unstore <item> or <number> YES
This will unstore the item as long as you have enough coins to do so.

{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~

0 Flash~
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
{R}                                   Flash
{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
Syntax: Flash

Flash lets you get in an "instant circle". In order to use it, you must
be wielding a dagger in one hand, and holding flash powder in the other.
Then type "flash" once you are already engaged and you will attempt
to get in an instant circle (Even if your opponent is attacking you!).
Flash powder is rare, so save this for important fights.

{d}[{R}+{d}]{B}-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-=-{d}[{R}+{d}]{N}
~
